# Preliminaries #

`œà ‚Ñì` denotes the type of h-set at level `‚Ñì`. Given an h-set `A`, we denote by
`‚ü¶ A ‚üß` its underlying type and by `isSet‚ü¶‚üß A` the proof that is is an h-set.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="Œ®"></a><a id="1547" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1547" class="Function">Œ®</a> <a id="1549" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1551" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1552" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1552" class="Bound">‚Ñì</a> <a id="1554" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1556" href="Agda.Primitive.html#523" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="1561" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1563" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="1565" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#1230" class="Primitive">Type</a> <a id="1570" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1571" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#1174" class="Primitive">‚Ñì-suc</a> <a id="1577" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1552" class="Bound">‚Ñì</a><a id="1578" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="1580" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1547" class="Function">Œ®</a> <a id="1582" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1582" class="Bound">‚Ñì</a> <a id="1584" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1586" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">Œ£[</a> <a id="1589" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1589" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="1591" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">‚àà</a> <a id="1593" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#1230" class="Primitive">Type</a> <a id="1598" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1582" class="Bound">‚Ñì</a> <a id="1600" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">]</a> <a id="1602" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#10036" class="Function">isSet</a> <a id="1608" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1589" class="Bound">A</a>

<a id="‚ü¶_‚üß"></a><a id="1611" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶_‚üß</a> <a id="1615" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1617" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1547" class="Function">Œ®</a> <a id="1619" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1337" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì</a> <a id="1621" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="1623" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#1230" class="Primitive">Type</a> <a id="1628" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1337" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì</a>
<a id="1630" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="1632" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1632" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="1634" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="1636" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="1638" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a> <a id="1640" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1642" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1632" class="Bound">A</a>

<a id="isSet‚ü¶‚üß"></a><a id="1645" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1645" class="Function">isSet‚ü¶‚üß</a> <a id="1653" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1655" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1656" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1656" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="1658" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1660" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1547" class="Function">Œ®</a> <a id="1662" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1337" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì</a><a id="1663" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1665" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="1667" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#10036" class="Function">isSet</a> <a id="1673" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1674" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#252" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="1678" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1656" class="Bound">A</a><a id="1679" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="1681" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1645" class="Function">isSet‚ü¶‚üß</a> <a id="1689" class="Symbol">(_</a> <a id="1692" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="1694" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1694" class="Bound">A-set</a><a id="1699" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1701" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1703" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1694" class="Bound">A-set</a>
</pre>
For convenience, we define some new versions of operators that work on
inhabitants of `Œ®` directly.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="_‚äç_"></a><a id="1823" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1823" class="Function Operator">_‚äç_</a> <a id="1827" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1829" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1547" class="Function">Œ®</a> <a id="1831" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1339" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì‚ÇÄ</a> <a id="1834" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="1836" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1547" class="Function">Œ®</a> <a id="1838" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1342" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì‚ÇÅ</a> <a id="1841" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="1843" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1547" class="Function">Œ®</a> <a id="1845" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1846" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#1202" class="Primitive">‚Ñì-max</a> <a id="1852" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1339" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì‚ÇÄ</a> <a id="1855" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1342" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì‚ÇÅ</a><a id="1857" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="1859" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1859" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="1861" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1823" class="Function Operator">‚äç</a> <a id="1863" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1863" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="1865" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1867" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1868" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="1870" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1859" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="1872" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a> <a id="1874" href="Cubical.Data.Sum.Base.html#226" class="Datatype Operator">‚äé</a> <a id="1876" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="1878" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1863" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="1880" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a><a id="1881" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1883" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="1885" href="Cubical.Data.Sum.Properties.html#3237" class="Function">isSetSum</a> <a id="1894" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1895" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1645" class="Function">isSet‚ü¶‚üß</a> <a id="1903" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1859" class="Bound">A</a><a id="1904" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="1906" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1907" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1645" class="Function">isSet‚ü¶‚üß</a> <a id="1915" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1863" class="Bound">B</a><a id="1916" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="‚Ñô"></a><a id="1919" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1919" class="Function">‚Ñô</a> <a id="1921" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1923" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1547" class="Function">Œ®</a> <a id="1925" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1337" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì</a> <a id="1927" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="1929" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#1230" class="Primitive">Type</a> <a id="1934" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1935" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#1174" class="Primitive">‚Ñì-suc</a> <a id="1941" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1337" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì</a><a id="1942" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="1944" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1919" class="Function">‚Ñô</a> <a id="1946" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1947" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1947" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="1949" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="1951" class="Symbol">_)</a> <a id="1954" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1956" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#955" class="Function">‚Ñô‚Ä≤</a> <a id="1959" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1947" class="Bound">A</a>

<a id="Fin"></a><a id="1962" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1962" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="1966" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1968" href="Cubical.Data.Nat.Base.html#222" class="Datatype">‚Ñï</a> <a id="1970" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="1972" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1547" class="Function">Œ®</a> <a id="1974" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#1145" class="Primitive">‚Ñì-zero</a>
<a id="1981" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1962" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="1985" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1985" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="1987" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="1989" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#428" class="Function">Fin‚Ä≤</a> <a id="1994" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1985" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="1996" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="1998" href="Cubical.Data.Fin.Properties.html#1444" class="Function">isSetFin</a>

<a id="ùüé"></a><a id="2008" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2008" class="Function">ùüé</a> <a id="2010" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2012" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="2014" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1962" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="2018" class="Number">1</a> <a id="2020" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a>
<a id="2022" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2008" class="Function">ùüé</a> <a id="2024" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2026" class="Number">0</a> <a id="2028" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="2030" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2031" class="Number">0</a> <a id="2033" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="2035" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#898" class="Function">refl</a><a id="2039" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
Definition of surjectivity.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="isSurjective"></a><a id="2083" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2083" class="Function">isSurjective</a> <a id="2096" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2098" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2099" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2099" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2101" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2103" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1547" class="Function">Œ®</a> <a id="2105" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1339" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì‚ÇÄ</a><a id="2107" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2109" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2110" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2110" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="2112" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2114" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1547" class="Function">Œ®</a> <a id="2116" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1342" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì‚ÇÅ</a><a id="2118" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2120" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="2122" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2123" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="2125" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2099" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2127" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a> <a id="2129" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="2131" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="2133" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2110" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="2135" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a><a id="2136" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2138" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="2140" href="Cubical.Foundations.HLevels.html#1500" class="Function">hProp</a> <a id="2146" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2147" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#1202" class="Primitive">‚Ñì-max</a> <a id="2153" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1339" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì‚ÇÄ</a> <a id="2156" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1342" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì‚ÇÅ</a><a id="2158" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="2160" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2083" class="Function">isSurjective</a> <a id="2173" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2173" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2175" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2175" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="2177" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2177" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="2179" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2181" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="2183" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2183" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="2185" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2187" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="2189" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2175" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="2191" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a><a id="2192" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2194" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="2196" href="Basis.html#6474" class="Datatype Operator">‚à•</a> <a id="2198" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">Œ£[</a> <a id="2201" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2201" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="2203" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">‚àà</a> <a id="2205" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="2207" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2173" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2209" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a> <a id="2211" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">]</a> <a id="2213" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2177" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="2215" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2201" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="2217" href="Agda.Builtin.Cubical.Path.html#381" class="Function Operator">‚â°</a> <a id="2219" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2183" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="2221" href="Basis.html#6474" class="Datatype Operator">‚à•</a><a id="2222" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2224" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="2226" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2246" class="Function">is-prop</a>
  <a id="2236" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="2246" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2246" class="Function">is-prop</a> <a id="2254" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2256" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#9981" class="Function">isProp</a> <a id="2263" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="2265" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2265" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="2267" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2269" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="2271" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2175" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="2273" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a><a id="2274" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2276" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="2278" href="Basis.html#6474" class="Datatype Operator">‚à•</a> <a id="2280" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">Œ£[</a> <a id="2283" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2283" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="2285" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">‚àà</a> <a id="2287" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="2289" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2173" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2291" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a> <a id="2293" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">]</a> <a id="2295" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2177" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="2297" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2283" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="2299" href="Agda.Builtin.Cubical.Path.html#381" class="Function Operator">‚â°</a> <a id="2301" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2265" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="2303" href="Basis.html#6474" class="Datatype Operator">‚à•</a><a id="2304" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="2310" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2246" class="Function">is-prop</a> <a id="2318" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2320" href="Cubical.Foundations.HLevels.html#14755" class="Function">isPropŒ†</a> <a id="2328" class="Symbol">Œª</a> <a id="2330" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2330" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="2332" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="2334" href="Basis.html#6561" class="Function">‚à•‚à•-prop</a> <a id="2342" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2343" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">Œ£[</a> <a id="2346" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2346" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="2348" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">‚àà</a> <a id="2350" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="2352" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2173" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2354" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a> <a id="2356" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">]</a> <a id="2358" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2177" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="2360" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2346" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="2362" href="Agda.Builtin.Cubical.Path.html#381" class="Function Operator">‚â°</a> <a id="2364" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2330" class="Bound">y</a><a id="2365" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
As we will talk about *subsets* i.e. subsets of inhabitants of a type that
satisfy a certain predicate, we write down a convenient notation for it.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="_restricted-to_"></a><a id="2529" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2529" class="Function Operator">_restricted-to_</a> <a id="2545" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2547" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2548" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2548" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2550" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2552" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1547" class="Function">Œ®</a> <a id="2554" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1337" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì</a><a id="2555" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2557" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="2559" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1919" class="Function">‚Ñô</a> <a id="2561" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2548" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2563" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="2565" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1547" class="Function">Œ®</a> <a id="2567" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1337" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì</a>
<a id="2569" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2529" class="Function Operator">_restricted-to_</a> <a id="2585" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2586" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2586" class="Bound">‚Ñì</a><a id="2587" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="2589" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2590" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2590" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2592" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="2594" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2594" class="Bound">A-set</a><a id="2599" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2601" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2601" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="2603" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2605" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2606" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">Œ£[</a> <a id="2609" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2609" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="2611" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">‚àà</a> <a id="2613" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2590" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2615" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">]</a> <a id="2617" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#715" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="2619" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2601" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="2621" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2609" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="2623" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#715" class="Function Operator">]</a><a id="2624" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2626" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="2628" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2647" class="Function">is-set</a>
  <a id="2637" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="2647" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2647" class="Function">is-set</a> <a id="2654" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2656" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#10036" class="Function">isSet</a> <a id="2662" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2663" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">Œ£[</a> <a id="2666" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2666" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="2668" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">‚àà</a> <a id="2670" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2590" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2672" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">]</a> <a id="2674" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#715" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="2676" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2601" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="2678" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2666" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="2680" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#715" class="Function Operator">]</a><a id="2681" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="2687" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2647" class="Function">is-set</a> <a id="2694" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2696" href="Cubical.Foundations.HLevels.html#12203" class="Function">isSetŒ£</a> <a id="2703" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2594" class="Bound">A-set</a> <a id="2709" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2710" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#13600" class="Function">isProp‚ÜíisSet</a> <a id="2723" href="Cubical.Foundations.Function.html#402" class="Function Operator">‚àò</a> <a id="2725" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#792" class="Function">isProp[]</a> <a id="2734" href="Cubical.Foundations.Function.html#402" class="Function Operator">‚àò</a> <a id="2736" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2601" class="Bound">U</a><a id="2737" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
`A ‚Ü† B` denotes the type of surjections from `A` to `B`.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="_‚Ü†_"></a><a id="2810" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2810" class="Function Operator">_‚Ü†_</a> <a id="2814" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2816" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1547" class="Function">Œ®</a> <a id="2818" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1339" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì‚ÇÄ</a> <a id="2821" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="2823" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1547" class="Function">Œ®</a> <a id="2825" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1342" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì‚ÇÅ</a> <a id="2828" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="2830" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1547" class="Function">Œ®</a> <a id="2832" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2833" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#1202" class="Primitive">‚Ñì-max</a> <a id="2839" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1339" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì‚ÇÄ</a> <a id="2842" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1342" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì‚ÇÅ</a><a id="2844" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="2846" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2846" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2848" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2810" class="Function Operator">‚Ü†</a> <a id="2850" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2850" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="2852" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="2854" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2855" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">Œ£[</a> <a id="2858" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2858" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="2860" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">‚àà</a> <a id="2862" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2863" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="2865" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2846" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2867" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a> <a id="2869" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="2871" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="2873" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2850" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="2875" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a><a id="2876" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2878" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">]</a> <a id="2880" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#715" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="2882" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2083" class="Function">isSurjective</a> <a id="2895" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2846" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2897" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2850" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="2899" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2858" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="2901" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#715" class="Function Operator">]</a><a id="2902" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2904" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="2906" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2924" class="Function">‚Ü†-set</a>
  <a id="2914" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="2924" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2924" class="Function">‚Ü†-set</a> <a id="2930" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="2932" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#10036" class="Function">isSet</a> <a id="2938" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2939" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">Œ£[</a> <a id="2942" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2942" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="2944" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">‚àà</a> <a id="2946" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2947" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="2949" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2846" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2951" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a> <a id="2953" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="2955" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="2957" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2850" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="2959" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a><a id="2960" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="2962" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">]</a> <a id="2964" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#715" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="2966" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2083" class="Function">isSurjective</a> <a id="2979" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2846" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="2981" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2850" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="2983" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2942" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="2985" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#715" class="Function Operator">]</a><a id="2986" class="Symbol">)</a>
    <a id="2992" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2924" class="Function">‚Ü†-set</a> <a id="2998" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3000" href="Cubical.Foundations.HLevels.html#12203" class="Function">isSetŒ£</a>
              <a id="3021" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3022" href="Cubical.Foundations.HLevels.html#15611" class="Function">isSetŒ†</a> <a id="3029" class="Symbol">(Œª</a> <a id="3032" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3032" class="Bound">_</a> <a id="3034" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="3036" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1645" class="Function">isSet‚ü¶‚üß</a> <a id="3044" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2850" class="Bound">B</a><a id="3045" class="Symbol">))</a>
              <a id="3062" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3063" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#13600" class="Function">isProp‚ÜíisSet</a> <a id="3076" href="Cubical.Foundations.Function.html#402" class="Function Operator">‚àò</a> <a id="3078" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#792" class="Function">isProp[]</a> <a id="3087" href="Cubical.Foundations.Function.html#402" class="Function Operator">‚àò</a> <a id="3089" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2083" class="Function">isSurjective</a> <a id="3102" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2846" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3104" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2850" class="Bound">B</a><a id="3105" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
A more suggestive notation for the underlying function of an inhabitant of `A ‚Ü†
B`.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="_$_"></a><a id="3205" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3205" class="Function Operator">_$_</a> <a id="3209" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3211" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#252" class="Field">fst</a>
</pre>
# Definition of Kuratowski-finiteness #

Our definition of [Kuratowski-finite][0] set `A` is: there exists a surjection
from `Fin n` (for some `n`) to `A`:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="isKFin"></a><a id="3385" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3385" class="Function">isKFin</a> <a id="3392" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3394" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3395" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3395" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3397" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3399" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1547" class="Function">Œ®</a> <a id="3401" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1337" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì</a><a id="3402" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3404" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="3406" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1919" class="Function">‚Ñô</a> <a id="3408" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3395" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3410" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="3412" href="Cubical.Foundations.HLevels.html#1500" class="Function">hProp</a> <a id="3418" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1337" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì</a>
<a id="3420" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3385" class="Function">isKFin</a> <a id="3427" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3427" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3429" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3429" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="3431" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="3435" href="Basis.html#6474" class="Datatype Operator">‚à•</a> <a id="3437" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">Œ£[</a> <a id="3440" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3440" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="3442" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">‚àà</a> <a id="3444" href="Cubical.Data.Nat.Base.html#222" class="Datatype">‚Ñï</a> <a id="3446" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">]</a> <a id="3448" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="3450" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1962" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="3454" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3440" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="3456" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2810" class="Function Operator">‚Ü†</a> <a id="3458" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3459" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3427" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3461" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2529" class="Function Operator">restricted-to</a> <a id="3475" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3429" class="Bound">U</a><a id="3476" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3478" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a> <a id="3480" href="Basis.html#6474" class="Datatype Operator">‚à•</a> <a id="3482" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="3484" href="Basis.html#6561" class="Function">‚à•‚à•-prop</a> <a id="3492" class="Symbol">_</a>

</pre>
The h-set of Kuratowski-finite sets is defined as:

<pre class="Agda"><a id="KFin"></a><a id="3672" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3672" class="Function">KFin</a> <a id="3677" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3679" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1547" class="Function">Œ®</a> <a id="3681" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1337" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì</a> <a id="3683" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="3685" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1547" class="Function">Œ®</a> <a id="3687" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3688" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#1174" class="Primitive">‚Ñì-suc</a> <a id="3694" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1337" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì</a><a id="3695" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="3697" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3672" class="Function">KFin</a> <a id="3702" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3702" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3704" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="3706" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3707" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">Œ£[</a> <a id="3710" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3710" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="3712" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">‚àà</a> <a id="3714" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1919" class="Function">‚Ñô</a> <a id="3716" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3702" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3718" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">]</a> <a id="3720" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#715" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="3722" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3385" class="Function">isKFin</a> <a id="3729" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3702" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3731" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3710" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="3733" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#715" class="Function Operator">]</a><a id="3734" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3736" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="3738" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3757" class="Function">is-set</a>
  <a id="3747" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="3757" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3757" class="Function">is-set</a> <a id="3764" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3766" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#10036" class="Function">isSet</a> <a id="3772" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3773" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">Œ£[</a> <a id="3776" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3776" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="3778" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">‚àà</a> <a id="3780" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1919" class="Function">‚Ñô</a> <a id="3782" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3702" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3784" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">]</a> <a id="3786" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#715" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="3788" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3385" class="Function">isKFin</a> <a id="3795" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3702" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3797" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3776" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="3799" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#715" class="Function Operator">]</a><a id="3800" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>
The following is nothing but a convenient notation for the irrelevance
of Kuratowski-finiteness proof to the equality.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="KFin-eq"></a><a id="3978" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3978" class="Function">KFin-eq</a> <a id="3986" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3988" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3989" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3989" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="3991" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3993" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1547" class="Function">Œ®</a> <a id="3995" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1337" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì</a><a id="3996" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="3998" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="4000" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4001" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4001" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="4003" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4003" class="Bound">V</a> <a id="4005" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4007" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="4009" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3672" class="Function">KFin</a> <a id="4014" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3989" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="4016" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a><a id="4017" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4019" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="4021" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#252" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="4025" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4001" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="4027" href="Agda.Builtin.Cubical.Path.html#381" class="Function Operator">‚â°</a> <a id="4029" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#252" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="4033" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4003" class="Bound">V</a> <a id="4035" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="4037" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4001" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="4039" href="Agda.Builtin.Cubical.Path.html#381" class="Function Operator">‚â°</a> <a id="4041" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4003" class="Bound">V</a>
<a id="4043" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3978" class="Function">KFin-eq</a> <a id="4051" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4051" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="4053" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4053" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="4055" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4055" class="Bound">V</a> <a id="4057" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4057" class="Bound">U=V</a> <a id="4061" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4063" href="Cubical.Data.Sigma.Properties.html#11948" class="Function">Œ£‚â°Prop</a> <a id="4070" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4071" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#792" class="Function">isProp[]</a> <a id="4080" href="Cubical.Foundations.Function.html#402" class="Function Operator">‚àò</a> <a id="4082" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3385" class="Function">isKFin</a> <a id="4089" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4051" class="Bound">A</a><a id="4090" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4092" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4057" class="Bound">U=V</a>

# Operations on Kuratowski-finite sets #

In this section, we assume a fixed h-set `A`.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="4198" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="4205" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4205" class="Module">_</a> <a id="4207" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4208" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4208" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="4210" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4212" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1547" class="Function">Œ®</a> <a id="4214" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1337" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì</a><a id="4215" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4217" class="Keyword">where</a>
</pre>
## The empty Kuratowski-finite set ##

<pre class="Agda">  <a id="4277" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4277" class="Function">‚àÖ</a> <a id="4279" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4281" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="4283" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3672" class="Function">KFin</a> <a id="4288" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4208" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="4290" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a>

      <a id="4394" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4340" class="Function">f</a>  <a id="4397" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4399" class="Symbol">(Œª</a> <a id="4402" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="4404" class="Symbol">(_</a> <a id="4407" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4409" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4409" class="Bound">n&lt;0</a><a id="4412" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4414" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="4416" href="Cubical.Data.Empty.Base.html#149" class="Function">rec</a> <a id="4420" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4421" href="Cubical.Data.Nat.Order.html#2823" class="Function">¬¨-&lt;-zero</a> <a id="4430" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4409" class="Bound">n&lt;0</a><a id="4433" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4435" class="Symbol">})</a> <a id="4438" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4440" class="Symbol">Œª</a> <a id="4442" class="Symbol">()</a>

  <a id="4448" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4448" class="Function">‚àÖ-uninhabited</a> <a id="4462" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4464" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="4466" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4208" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="4468" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2529" class="Function Operator">restricted-to</a> <a id="4482" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#252" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="4486" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4277" class="Function">‚àÖ</a> <a id="4488" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a> <a id="4490" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="4492" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#715" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="4494" href="Cubical.Functions.Logic.html#2853" class="Function">‚ä•</a> <a id="4496" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#715" class="Function Operator">]</a>

## Singleton Kuratowski-finite set ##

<pre class="Agda">  <a id="4577" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4577" class="Function">single</a> <a id="4584" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4586" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="4588" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4208" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="4590" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a> <a id="4592" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="4594" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1919" class="Function">‚Ñô</a> <a id="4596" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4208" class="Bound">A</a>

  <a id="4644" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4644" class="Function">Œ∑</a> <a id="4646" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4648" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="4650" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4208" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="4652" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a> <a id="4654" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="4656" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="4658" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3672" class="Function">KFin</a> <a id="4663" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4208" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="4665" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a>
  <a id="4669" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4644" class="Function">Œ∑</a> <a id="4671" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4671" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4673" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="4676" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4577" class="Function">single</a> <a id="4683" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4671" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4685" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4687" href="Basis.html#6508" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚à£</a> <a id="4689" class="Number">1</a> <a id="4691" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4693" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4769" class="Function">f</a> <a id="4695" href="Basis.html#6508" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚à£</a>
    <a id="4701" class="Keyword">where</a>
      <a id="4713" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4713" class="Function">‚ÅÖx‚ÅÜ</a> <a id="4717" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4719" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1547" class="Function">Œ®</a> <a id="4721" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4214" class="Bound">‚Ñì</a>
   <a id="4726" class="Argument"> </a>  <a id="4729" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4713" class="Function">‚ÅÖx‚ÅÜ</a> <a id="4733" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4735" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4208" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="4737" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2529" class="Function Operator">restricted-to</a> <a id="4751" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4752" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4577" class="Function">single</a> <a id="4759" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4671" class="Bound">x</a><a id="4760" class="Symbol">)</a>

      <a id="4769" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4769" class="Function">f</a> <a id="4771" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4773" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="4775" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1962" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="4779" class="Number">1</a> <a id="4781" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2810" class="Function Operator">‚Ü†</a> <a id="4783" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4713" class="Function">‚ÅÖx‚ÅÜ</a> <a id="4787" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a>
      <a id="4795" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4769" class="Function">f</a> <a id="4797" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4799" class="Symbol">(Œª</a> <a id="4802" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4802" class="Bound">_</a> <a id="4804" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="4806" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4671" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4808" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4810" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#898" class="Function">refl</a><a id="4814" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4816" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4818" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4847" class="Function">surj</a>
        <a id="4831" class="Keyword">where</a>
          <a id="4847" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4847" class="Function">surj</a> <a id="4852" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4854" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#715" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="4856" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2083" class="Function">isSurjective</a> <a id="4869" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4870" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1962" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="4874" class="Number">1</a><a id="4875" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4877" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4713" class="Function">‚ÅÖx‚ÅÜ</a> <a id="4881" class="Symbol">(Œª</a> <a id="4884" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4884" class="Bound">_</a> <a id="4886" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="4888" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4671" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="4890" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4892" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#898" class="Function">refl</a><a id="4896" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4898" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#715" class="Function Operator">]</a>
          <a id="4910" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4847" class="Function">surj</a> <a id="4915" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4916" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4916" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="4918" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4920" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4920" class="Bound">p</a><a id="4921" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4923" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="4925" href="Basis.html#6508" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚à£</a> <a id="4927" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2008" class="Function">ùüé</a> <a id="4929" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="4931" href="Cubical.Data.Sigma.Properties.html#11948" class="Function">Œ£‚â°Prop</a> <a id="4938" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4939" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#792" class="Function">isProp[]</a> <a id="4948" href="Cubical.Foundations.Function.html#402" class="Function Operator">‚àò</a> <a id="4950" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4577" class="Function">single</a> <a id="4957" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4671" class="Bound">x</a><a id="4958" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4960" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4920" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="4962" href="Basis.html#6508" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">‚à£</a>
</pre>
## Union of two Kuratowski-finite sets ##

Some arithmetic lemmata. It is likely that these have either been proven in
`cubical` or can be proven more efficiently using other lemmata that have been
proven in `cubical`. If you have any suggestions please make a PR.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="o&lt;m‚Üío&lt;m+n"></a><a id="5243" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#5243" class="Function">o&lt;m‚Üío&lt;m+n</a> <a id="5253" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5255" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5256" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#5256" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="5258" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#5258" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="5260" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#5260" class="Bound">o</a> <a id="5262" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5264" href="Cubical.Data.Nat.Base.html#222" class="Datatype">‚Ñï</a><a id="5265" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5267" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="5269" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#5260" class="Bound">o</a> <a id="5271" href="Cubical.Data.Nat.Order.html#554" class="Function Operator">&lt;</a> <a id="5273" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#5256" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="5275" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="5277" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#5260" class="Bound">o</a> <a id="5279" href="Cubical.Data.Nat.Order.html#554" class="Function Operator">&lt;</a> <a id="5281" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5282" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#5256" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="5284" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#325" class="Primitive Operator">+</a> <a id="5286" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#5258" class="Bound">n</a><a id="5287" class="Symbol">)</a>

We will often be interested in whether `m < n` or not.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="_‚â§?_"></a><a id="5967" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#5967" class="Function Operator">_‚â§?_</a> <a id="5972" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5974" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5975" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#5975" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="5977" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#5977" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="5979" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5981" href="Cubical.Data.Nat.Base.html#222" class="Datatype">‚Ñï</a><a id="5982" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5984" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="5986" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5987" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#5975" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="5989" href="Cubical.Data.Nat.Order.html#554" class="Function Operator">&lt;</a> <a id="5991" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#5977" class="Bound">n</a><a id="5992" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5994" href="Cubical.Data.Sum.Base.html#226" class="Datatype Operator">‚äé</a> <a id="5996" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5997" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#5977" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="5999" href="Cubical.Data.Nat.Order.html#504" class="Function Operator">‚â§</a> <a id="6001" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#5975" class="Bound">m</a><a id="6002" class="Symbol">)</a>

### `Fin (m + n) ‚â° Fin m ‚äé Fin n` ###

The following fact is crucial for the definition of union for Kuratowski-finite
sets.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="Fin+‚âÉFin‚äéFin"></a><a id="7385" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#7385" class="Function">Fin+‚âÉFin‚äéFin</a> <a id="7398" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7400" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7401" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#7401" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="7403" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#7403" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="7405" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7407" href="Cubical.Data.Nat.Base.html#222" class="Datatype">‚Ñï</a><a id="7408" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7410" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="7412" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="7414" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1962" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="7418" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7419" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#7401" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="7421" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#325" class="Primitive Operator">+</a> <a id="7423" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#7403" class="Bound">n</a><a id="7424" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7426" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a> <a id="7428" href="Agda.Builtin.Cubical.Path.html#381" class="Function Operator">‚â°</a> <a id="7430" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="7432" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1962" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="7436" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#7401" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="7438" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a> <a id="7440" href="Cubical.Data.Sum.Base.html#226" class="Datatype Operator">‚äé</a> <a id="7442" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="7444" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1962" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="7448" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#7403" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="7450" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a>

<a id="8570" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#8509" class="Function">Fin-sum-lemma‚Ä≤</a> <a id="8585" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#8585" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="8587" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#8587" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="8589" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8591" href="Cubical.Data.Sigma.Properties.html#11948" class="Function">Œ£‚â°Prop</a> <a id="8598" class="Symbol">(Œª</a> <a id="8601" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#8601" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="8603" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="8605" href="Cubical.Foundations.HLevels.html#4402" class="Function">isPropIsSet</a> <a id="8617" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8618" class="Argument">A</a> <a id="8620" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8622" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#8601" class="Bound">A</a><a id="8623" class="Symbol">})</a> <a id="8626" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8627" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#7385" class="Function">Fin+‚âÉFin‚äéFin</a> <a id="8640" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#8585" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="8642" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#8587" class="Bound">n</a><a id="8643" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
Let us first define the union of two subsets.

               <a id="10481" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10482" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#955" class="Function">sym</a> <a id="10486" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10487" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#8509" class="Function">Fin-sum-lemma‚Ä≤</a> <a id="10502" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#9137" class="Bound">m</a> <a id="10504" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#9147" class="Bound">n</a><a id="10505" class="Symbol">))</a>
               <a id="10523" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10524" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#9256" class="Function">h</a> <a id="10526" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10528" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#9478" class="Function">h-surj</a><a id="10534" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
# Induction principle of Kuratowski-finite sets #

We prove in this section the induction principle of Kuratowski-finite sets:

to show that _all_ Kuratowski-finite sets satisfy some predicate $P$, it
suffices to show

  1. $‚àÖ$ satisfies P;
  2. $\left\{ x \right\}$ satisfies $P$, for every $x$; and
  3. given two Kuratowski-finite sets $U$ and $V$ satisfying $P$,
     the union $U ‚à™ V$ satisfies $P$.

The proof of this induction principle is given at the very end of this section.

If a surjection exists from `Fin 1` to `A`, `A` is contractible.

    <a id="11960" class="Keyword">where</a>
      <a id="11972" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#11972" class="Function">U-contr</a> <a id="11980" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11982" href="Cubical.Foundations.Prelude.html#9917" class="Function">isContr</a> <a id="11990" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="11992" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#11747" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="11994" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2529" class="Function Operator">restricted-to</a> <a id="12008" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#11876" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="12010" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a>
      <a id="12018" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#11972" class="Function">U-contr</a> <a id="12026" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12028" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#11104" class="Function">KFin1‚ÜíisContr</a> <a id="12042" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12043" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#11747" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="12045" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2529" class="Function Operator">restricted-to</a> <a id="12059" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#11876" class="Bound">U</a><a id="12060" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12062" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#11878" class="Bound">f</a>

      <a id="12071" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#12071" class="Function">centre</a> <a id="12078" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12080" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#252" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="12084" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#11972" class="Function">U-contr</a>

    <a id="12685" class="Keyword">where</a>
      <a id="12697" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#12697" class="Function">NTS‚ÇÄ</a> <a id="12702" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12704" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#252" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="12708" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#12589" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="12710" href="Cubical.Foundations.Powerset.html#800" class="Function Operator">‚äÜ</a> <a id="12712" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#252" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="12716" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12717" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4277" class="Function">‚àÖ</a> <a id="12719" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#11747" class="Bound">A</a><a id="12720" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="12728" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#12697" class="Function">NTS‚ÇÄ</a> <a id="12733" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#12733" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="12735" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#12735" class="Bound">x‚ààU</a> <a id="12739" class="Symbol">=</a>
        <a id="12749" href="Basis.html#6619" class="Function">‚à•‚à•-rec</a> <a id="12756" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12757" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#792" class="Function">isProp[]</a> <a id="12766" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12767" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#252" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="12771" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12772" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4277" class="Function">‚àÖ</a> <a id="12774" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#11747" class="Bound">A</a><a id="12775" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12777" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#12733" class="Bound">x</a><a id="12778" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="12781" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12782" href="Cubical.Data.Empty.Base.html#149" class="Function">rec</a> <a id="12786" href="Cubical.Foundations.Function.html#402" class="Function Operator">‚àò</a> <a id="12788" href="Cubical.Data.Fin.Base.html#1647" class="Function">¬¨Fin0</a> <a id="12794" href="Cubical.Foundations.Function.html#402" class="Function Operator">‚àò</a> <a id="12796" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#252" class="Field">fst</a><a id="12799" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12801" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12802" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#12596" class="Bound">f-surj</a> <a id="12809" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12810" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#12733" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="12812" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12814" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#12735" class="Bound">x‚ààU</a><a id="12817" class="Symbol">))</a>

      <a id="12827" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#12827" class="Function">NTS‚ÇÅ</a> <a id="12832" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12834" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#252" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="12838" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12839" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4277" class="Function">‚àÖ</a> <a id="12841" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#11747" class="Bound">A</a><a id="12842" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12844" href="Cubical.Foundations.Powerset.html#800" class="Function Operator">‚äÜ</a> <a id="12846" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#252" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="12850" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#12589" class="Bound">U</a>
      <a id="12858" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#12827" class="Function">NTS‚ÇÅ</a> <a id="12863" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#12863" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="12865" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#12865" class="Bound">x‚àà‚àÖ</a> <a id="12869" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12871" href="Cubical.Data.Empty.Base.html#149" class="Function">rec</a> <a id="12875" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12876" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4448" class="Function">‚àÖ-uninhabited</a> <a id="12890" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#11747" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="12892" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12893" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#12863" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="12895" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12897" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#12865" class="Bound">x‚àà‚àÖ</a><a id="12900" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="12906" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#12906" class="Function Operator">_+1</a> <a id="12910" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12912" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12913" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#12913" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="12915" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12917" href="Cubical.Data.Nat.Base.html#222" class="Datatype">‚Ñï</a><a id="12918" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="12920" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="12922" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="12924" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1962" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="12928" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#12913" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="12930" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a> <a id="12932" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="12934" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="12936" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1962" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="12940" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12941" href="Agda.Builtin.Nat.html#223" class="InductiveConstructor">suc</a> <a id="12945" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#12913" class="Bound">n</a><a id="12946" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12948" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a>
  <a id="12952" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12953" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#12953" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="12955" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12957" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#12957" class="Bound">k&lt;n</a><a id="12960" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12962" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#12906" class="Function Operator">+1</a> <a id="12965" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12967" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#12953" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="12969" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12971" href="Cubical.Data.Nat.Order.html#1046" class="Function">suc-‚â§-suc</a> <a id="12981" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12982" href="Cubical.Data.Nat.Order.html#3387" class="Function">&lt;-weaken</a> <a id="12991" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#12957" class="Bound">k&lt;n</a><a id="12994" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
This is the real content of the proof which amounts taking a Kuratowski-finite
set $U$ of size `n ‚â• 2` and decomposing it as $U = \{ x \} ‚à™ U‚Ä≤$.

## The proof of the induction principle ##

<pre class="Agda"><a id="K-ind"></a><a id="16290" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#16290" class="Function">K-ind</a> <a id="16296" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16298" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16299" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#16299" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="16301" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16303" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1547" class="Function">Œ®</a> <a id="16305" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1337" class="Generalizable">‚Ñì</a><a id="16306" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="16314" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="16316" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16317" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#16317" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="16319" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16321" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1919" class="Function">‚Ñô</a> <a id="16323" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16324" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#3672" class="Function">KFin</a> <a id="16329" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#16299" class="Bound">A</a><a id="16330" class="Symbol">))</a>
      <a id="16339" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="16341" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#715" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="16343" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#16317" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="16345" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16346" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4277" class="Function">‚àÖ</a> <a id="16348" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#16299" class="Bound">A</a><a id="16349" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16351" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#715" class="Function Operator">]</a>
      <a id="16359" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="16361" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="16363" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#16363" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="16365" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16367" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#252" class="Field">fst</a> <a id="16371" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#16299" class="Bound">A</a><a id="16372" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16374" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="16376" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#715" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="16378" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#16317" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="16380" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16381" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#4644" class="Function">Œ∑</a> <a id="16383" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#16299" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="16385" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#16363" class="Bound">x</a><a id="16386" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16388" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#715" class="Function Operator">]</a><a id="16389" class="Symbol">)</a>

    <a id="16582" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#16582" class="Function">nts</a> <a id="16586" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="16588" href="Cubical.Core.Primitives.html#6302" class="Function">Œ£-syntax</a> <a id="16597" href="Cubical.Data.Nat.Base.html#222" class="Datatype">‚Ñï</a> <a id="16599" class="Symbol">(Œª</a> <a id="16602" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#16602" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="16604" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="16606" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚ü¶</a> <a id="16608" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1962" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="16612" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#16602" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="16614" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2810" class="Function Operator">‚Ü†</a> <a id="16616" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16617" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#16512" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="16619" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#2529" class="Function Operator">restricted-to</a> <a id="16633" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#16523" class="Bound">U</a><a id="16634" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16636" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#1611" class="Function Operator">‚üß</a><a id="16637" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16639" class="Symbol">‚Üí</a> <a id="16641" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#715" class="Function Operator">[</a> <a id="16643" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#16514" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="16645" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16646" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#16523" class="Bound">U</a> <a id="16648" href="Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#236" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="16650" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#16527" class="Bound">p</a><a id="16651" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16653" href="KuratowskiFinite.html#715" class="Function Operator">]</a>
